These changes provide powerful protections that make Mimikatz almost worthless.</p><p id="ac0f" class="pw-post-body-paragraph oz pa jr pb b pc pd pe pf pg ph pi pj hr pk pl pm hu pn po pp hx pq pr ps pt is bk">2.
